< Review>
Sky is a wonderful human being! She is understanding of what your hair goals are and it's easy to chat, and feel at ease while being taken care of. She listened to what I was describing and did not struggle to understand what I wanted in a haircut.

My problem with my experience was I walked in with an idea of what I wanted with hair color but walked out with something completely different. I was hoping for light brown roots transitioning into pastel pink on the bottom (my hair is pastel pink already).

Since my last stylist used a different kind of chemical, Sky was not able to remove the staining it created from that previous visit, so instead of the light brown I wanted at my roots, we had to cover it up with a dark purple instead.

I appreciate the transparency and communication Sky made with me throughout the process and our limited options to pivot. We unfortunately trimmed much of the remaining pink after dying which I did not account for when we made the initial suggestions on where each color would start during the beginning. After washing out the dark purple, a lot of it also slid down to the bottom pink, darkening my overall look. Majority of my hair is purple now which is a bummer since it doesn't resonate with who I am. :(

Asian hair is tough to get right when it comes to coloring. Asian hair is also mad expensive to color--bottom line is I paid a hefty price for something I didn't want. But hey, it was a service provided to me so I'll respect that and pay it. It looks cool but just not me.

The intention of my visit was to begin transitioning from my pastel into a more natural look with the brown. This took me the opposite direction with the purple. I was trying to convince myself to like it more than I really did in the moment as a coping mechanism I suppose because the visit took such an unexpected turn. It's going to take some time to get used to it and I'll admit I am kind of in shock still, but want to treat this review as fairly as possible.

UPDATE
I'm very displeased because after my first wash I was in shock that any of the remaining pink is completely obliterated. As my 2nd and 3rd wash went on, the whole thing turned less magenta and more and more purple. I wish I was warned the purple would take over any remnants of pink or else I would have urged to pursue a different route. I am very sad about it because the original pastel pink took years to achieve and costed me thousands, only to get completely annihilated. I basically paid $500 on this service for something I don't want, it honestly feels so violating. Sigh.< /Review>

<rating>5</rating>< Text>
After a self-inflicted quarantine color fiasco, I was left with tangerine orange hair. By good luck, I contacted BIBO the day they reopened, and even though her schedule was quite full, Susie was quick to respond. She was kind enough to do my consult via video call, and incredibly sensitive to my needs and schedule. She went WAY over the call of customer service - even extending her hours to meet my schedule, so I could look normal again as soon as possible. Her color correction was on point, and she got me back to a natural-looking state in one appointment - and she was faster than any treatment I've ever had, previously! "Blow In, Blow Out" is the absolute truth - I cannot believe how amazing my service and experience with her was - and she's an awesome person, on top of it! Absolutely worth every penny - she even styled me so I could arrive at my next appointment polished, and feeling great. Susie is a true professional - her passion for truly informed haircare and technique is apparent, and I'm super excited to return for a Calligraphy haircut (she's the only provider in the Bay Area). BIBO has earned my loyalty, for sure - and I can't recommend Susie enough!< /Text>

I cannot speak highly enough of this Salon! The stylist who did my hair, Leahla in was excellent in her skills and expertise in regards to her understanding of hair design and health! Not only was she a highly skilled  hair stylist/ designer, but she was extremely easy-going and comfortable to talk to!

The other bridesmaids where thrilled with their stylists Allie, who thrilled with her expertise of color and tone, in regards to Bethany's complexion. Alice was equally thrilled with the stylist flair of Corina!

The Bride Alison was thrilled with the excellent job that her team Haili and Jezabel ! She had her hair dyed and purchased extensions to match the length and color! She was so thrilled with how her hair came out! Her makeup, done by the very talented team, was beautiful and everyone at the wedding remarked on how beautiful the bride was!

The lady at the front desk was extremely helpful in helping us navigate the keurig and the side table of snacks, fruit, cheese and crack and fruit. She also noticed when my hair fell out of place and we quickly refinished the up-do toward the end of the session. How very observant and helpful everyone was!<//Text>

< Review>
What a cool spot! If you are a giants fan (or a baseball fan...or even just a sports fan) this is a must visit restaurant. After living in the Midwest one of my main complaints about SF is the lack of sports bars or restaurants. I have finally found my place!

Pine tar is covered in authentic giants memorabilia (think of your favorite giants player from the past 30 years. I guarantee his game used bat is hanging somewhere in this restaurant) and TVs for watching the game, not to mention the jerseys, vintage photos, and autographs. The food is great, service is quick, and staff is friendly. So happy this place opened in SOMA and can't wait to become a regular. This place just opened so I would recommend visiting now before the word gets out.< /Review>

Our vet retired during the pandemic, and recently, Darwin was having some type of reaction that was causing itchiness and redness throughout his body - he was absolutely miserable. This wasn't the first time it happened, and previously, he would get prescribed prednisone and nothing more. It worked short term - but it would happen again. <review>My friends and I wanted some good korean food and went here for sul lung tang (mixed beef soup) and samgetang (whole chicken soup). Service was sweet and bomb and the layout is very traditional korean style. Their side dishes were sooo good. We especially asked more of the spicy pickled radish cause it went so well with our soups. Friends loved it and I want to go back to try the sul lung tang.<//review></record></dataset><record>
<text>Great food okay price . Place is very small so order out and enjoy at home. The service might seem unfriendly to none Koreans. But they're  old school Koreans so no small talk don't get offended.  Customer services means get your food as quick as possible and maybe a smile. They might have a distressed look on there face while taking your order but trust me it isn't you they're stressing on something else. Food is AWESOME . Rice and side orders complimentary with most soups.  And the Kim chee is on point. I've only had soups but there noodles look good I'm gonna try it this week . FYI :  before you leave grab a menu so you can order on the phone next time and have it ready when you get there.<//text>< rating>

< text>
The Sul Lang Tang Soup was just what i needed as i was feeling body aches, chills and an onset of a fever.

This is my new go-to Sul Lang Tang place. The broth is delicious: milky-color flavored with the bones that have been stewing for hours. the service is great! They also give a variety of banchan.

I don't want to share this gem because i don't want there to be a wait the next time i go -- but i do wish for others to know how good the food tastes here.

There is a parking lot but often times -- it is crowded. Thank goodness it is not LA and there is ample parking on the street as well.</text>

<Text>Looking for a spot to grab lunch in Redlands, to yelp I go... Mill Creek Bar-B-Q was a pleasant surprise.  My husband and I split a pull pork and fries.  I love the fact that they have different Bar-B-Q sauces that you can apply yourself.  My hubby had to try them all...

<Pics>None</Pics><time>1387751968895<//time>< Review>
We decided to get breakfast there because we saw some reviews online and we also read some that stated that they just got remodeled on restaurants impossible. We like that show so we were pretty excited to go there and check it out. Things started out pretty well it was obvious that it was professionally remodeled, and it looked great. When we ordered things started to go downhill. We both ordered breakfast and we are told that they're out of hashbrowns so we had a get tater tots instead. They want to breakfast team one of them actually had hashbrowns and we got them to get us more hashbrowns for the other plate. One dish we ordered was the veggie omelette which was actually pretty good, however the hashbrowns were pretty bland. The other dish we ordered was a breakfast with potatoes eggs and biscuits and gravy, which we're told there out of biscuits then the guy tried to get us to get toast with gravy. Are you serious toast with gravy come on? I ended up getting French toast instead which was pretty bland my eggs were supposed to be over easy they came out more like over medium. While we sat and ate our breakfast we could tell that there were other tables I had issues with their food. Overall we are not really that impressed and don't think will be back for a long time. Chef Robert Irvine along with restaurants impossible was only there two weeks ago and I think someone needs to let him know that he needs to go back and fix this place. The episode is going to air in March 2014, and I hope they get their act together by then or else they're not gonna be able to watch their own show.< /Review>
